// =============================================================================
// Function Class: Show/Hide product promotions & special offers link
// =============================================================================

function showElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'visible';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'block';
    }
  }
}
function hideElement(id) {
  var elm = document.getElementById(id);
  if (elm) {
    elm.style.visibility = 'hidden';
    if (elm.getAttribute('name') == 'heroQuickPromoDiv') {
      elm.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }
}
function showHideElement(h_id, div_id) {
  var hiddenTag = document.getElementById(h_id);
  if (hiddenTag) {
    showElement(div_id);
  } else {
    hideElement(div_id);
  }
}

    var escChar = String.fromCharCode(0x5c);
    function isValidEmail(emailAddress) {
        //If email not supported or invalid email address return false
        if ( parseInt("") || (emailAddress && typeof emailAddress !== "string" )) {
            return false;
        }

        // validating only from @ to end
        var validator = new RegExp(escChar + "w+@[" + escChar +"w" + escChar + "-+_]+?" + escChar + ".[" + escChar + "w" + escChar + "-+_]+");
        return emailAddress.match( validator ) != null;
    }
    
    function isValidPhone(phoneNumber) {
        //If sms not supported or no input return false
        if ( parseInt("") || !phoneNumber ) {
            return false;
        }

        var validator = new RegExp("^([0-9" + escChar + "(" + escChar + ")" + escChar + "/" + escChar + "+" + escChar + "-]*)$");
        var digitsOnly = phoneNumber.replace(/D/g, '');
        return digitsOnly.length >= 9 && digitsOnly.length < 20 && phoneNumber.match(validator) != null; 
    }
    
    function appendCountryCode(phoneNumber) {
        var countryCode = "";
        if ( countryCode && isValidPhone(phoneNumber) && !phoneNumber.match(/^\+/g) ) {
            phoneNumber = countryCode + phoneNumber;
        }
        return phoneNumber;
    }
    
    var successMessage = "The app is on the way!";
    var processError = "";
    var popupOptions = {
        title: "Get the free Kindle Reading App",
        localContent: "#kcpAppsPopOverDialog_",
        closeEventInclude: "CLICK_OUTSIDE",
        modal: "true",
        closeText: "Close",
        width: 760,
        onShow: function() {
            jQuery.ajax({
                url: '/gp/digital/fiona/ajax/reftagCall.html/ref=kcpapp_pb_atf?pf_rd_p=1958077202&pf_rd_s=kcpAppsWidget&pf_rd_t=201&pf_rd_i=0321751043&pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_r=0CXWM3AES9PQ177J93Z1',
                dataType: 'json',
                cache: false,
                type: 'GET'
            });
        }
    }

    amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() {
    //Remove the existing bindings if Any. Because multiple widgets on same page will create multiple popovers.
    kcpAppBaseObj_.find('.kcpAppsPopOver').removeAmazonPopoverTrigger();
    kcpAppBaseObj_.find('.kcpAppsPopOver').amazonPopoverTrigger(popupOptions);
    });
    
    function setSelector(element, downloadMessage, downloadUrl, tinyImage, emailSmartLink, smsSmartLink){
      emailSmartLink_ = emailSmartLink;
      smsSmartLink_ = smsSmartLink;
      kcpAppDialogObj_.find(".kcpAppDeviceUL .selectedElement").addClass("invisible");
      kcpAppDialogObj_.find(".kcpAppDeviceUL .kcpAppSelected").removeClass("kcpAppSelected");
      kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess, .kcpAppDeliveryError').html("");
      jQuery(element).find(".selectedElement").removeClass("invisible");
      jQuery(element).find(".kcpAppDeviceListItem .mask img").addClass( "kcpAppSelected" );
      
      kcpAppDialogObj_.find("#kcpAppDownloadMessage").html(downloadMessage);
      if(tinyImage && downloadUrl){
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find("#kcpAppTinyImage").attr("src",tinyImage );
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find("#kcpAppDirectDownloadLink").show();
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find("#kcpAppDirectURL").attr("href", downloadUrl);
      } else{
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find("#kcpAppDirectDownloadLink").hide();
      }
    }

        kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppRecipient').unbind('keypress'); //Unbind previous clicks to avoid duplicate bindings.
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppRecipient').keypress(function(e){
            if (e.which == 13){
                kcpAppDialogObj_.find(".kcpAppSendButton").click();
            }
        });
        
        if(jQuery.browser && jQuery.browser.msie){
            kcpAppDialogObj_.find('[placeholder]').focus(function() {
              var input = jQuery(this);
              if (input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                input.val('');
                input.removeClass('placeholder');
              }
            }).blur(function() {
              var input = jQuery(this);
              if (input.val() == '' || input.val() == input.attr('placeholder')) {
                input.addClass('placeholder');
                input.val(input.attr('placeholder'));
              }
            }).blur();
        }
        
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find(".kcpAppSendButton").unbind("click"); //Unbind previous clicks to avoid duplicate bindings.
        kcpAppDialogObj_.find(".kcpAppSendButton").bind("click", function(){
           var recipient = kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppRecipient').val();
           var inputData = {
            "recipient" : appendCountryCode(recipient),
            "downloadLink" : (emailSmartLink_) ? emailSmartLink_ : "http://www.amazon.com/gp/kindle/kcpApp.html",
            "toJSON" : "1"
           };
           if(isValidEmail(recipient)){
               inputData['communicationType'] = 'email';
               submitRTERequest(inputData);
           } else if(isValidPhone(recipient)){
               inputData['communicationType'] = 'sms';
               submitRTERequest(inputData);
               if(smsSmartLink_){
                 inputData[downloadLink] = smsSmartLink_;
               }
           } else {
               kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess, .kcpAppDeliveryError').html("");
               kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryError').html("Invalid input, Please provide valid Email or Mobile no.");
           }
        });  

      function submitRTERequest(input){
        jQuery.extend(input,csrfParamsJson);
        jQuery.ajax({
                url: "/gp/digital/fiona/ajax/send-email-or-sms.html/ref=kcpapp_snt_pb_atf",
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "json",
                data: input,
                beforeSend:function(){
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess, .kcpAppDeliveryError').html("");
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryInProgress').html('<div style="text-align:center"><img src="http://g-ecx.images-amazon.com/images/G/01/kindle/www/myk/icon_spinner._V192549371_.gif" /> Processing your request... </div>');
                },
                success:function(data){
                  kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryInProgress').html("");
                  if(typeof(data) == "string"){
                      data=JSON.parse(data);
                  }
                  if(data && data.status == 1) {
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess').html( successMessage + ((input.communicationType == 'email') ? " Please check your email." : " Please check your mobile phone.") +".");
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppRecipient').val("");
                  } else {
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess, .kcpAppDeliveryError').html("");
                    data['message'] = (data.status) ? "Invalid Request" : data.message;
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryError').html(((data.message) ? data.message : processError));
                  }
                },
                error:function(){
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryInProgress').html("");
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliverySuccess, .kcpAppDeliveryError').html("");
                    kcpAppDialogObj_.find('.kcpAppDeliveryError').html(processError);
                }
            });
      }
      
      jQuery.ajax({
            url: "/gp/digital/fiona/ajax/reftagCall.html/ref=kcpapp_load_pb_atf",
            dataType: 'json',
            cache: false,
            type: 'GET'
      });
    });
    
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
FT_showAndInCountdown = false;
FT_HourString = "hr";
FT_HoursString = "hrs";
FT_MinuteString = "min";
FT_MinutesString = "mins";
FT_AndString = "and";

function getElementsByClassNameCustom(className) {
    var selectedElements = [];
    if (document.getElementsByClassName) {
        selectedElements = document.getElementsByClassName(className);
    } else if (document.querySelectorAll) {
        selectedElements = document.querySelectorAll("." + className);
    }
    return selectedElements;
}

var FT_CurrentDisplayMin;
var clientServerTimeDrift;
var firstTimeUpdate = true;

var countdownElements = getElementsByClassNameCustom("ftCountdownClass");
if (countdownElements.length < 1) {
    countdownElements.push(document.getElementById("ftCountdown"));
}

function getTimeRemainingString( hours, minutes )
{
  var hourString   =  ( hours == 1 ? FT_HourString : FT_HoursString );
  var minuteString =  ( minutes  == 1 ? FT_MinuteString : FT_MinutesString );
  if (hours == 0) {
    return minutes + " " + minuteString;
  }
  if (minutes == 0) {
    return hours + " " + hourString;
  }
  if (FT_showAndInCountdown) {
    return hours + " " + hourString + " " + FT_AndString + " " + minutes + " " + minuteString;
  } else {
    return hours + " " + hourString + " " + minutes + " " + minuteString;
  }
}
function FT_displayCountdown(forceUpdate)
{
  var FT_remainSeconds = FT_givenSeconds - FT_actualSeconds;
  if (FT_remainSeconds < 1 && document.getElementById("fast-track")) {
    document.getElementById("fast-track").style.display = "none";
  }
  var FT_secondsPerDay = 24 * 60 * 60;
  var FT_daysLong = FT_remainSeconds / FT_secondsPerDay;
  var FT_days = Math.floor(FT_daysLong);
  var FT_hoursLong = (FT_daysLong - FT_days) * 24;
  var FT_hours = Math.floor(FT_hoursLong);
  var FT_minsLong = (FT_hoursLong - FT_hours) * 60;
  var FT_mins = Math.floor(FT_minsLong);
  var FT_secsLong = (FT_minsLong - FT_mins) * 60;
  var FT_secs = Math.floor(FT_secsLong);
  if (FT_days > 0) {
    FT_hours = (FT_days * 24) + FT_hours;
  }
  setTimeout(FT_getTime, 1000);
  var ftCountdown = getTimeRemainingString( FT_hours, FT_mins );
  if (countdownElements.length) {
    if (FT_CurrentDisplayMin != FT_mins || forceUpdate || firstTimeUpdate) {
      var i = 0, countdownElement;
      while (countdownElement = countdownElements[i++]) {
        countdownElement.innerHTML = ftCountdown;
      }
      FT_CurrentDisplayMin = FT_mins;
      firstTimeUpdate = false;
    }
  }
}

function FT_getCountdown(secondsLeft)
{
  var FT_currentTime = new Date();
  var FT_currentHours = FT_currentTime.getHours();
  var FT_currentMins = FT_currentTime.getMinutes();
  var FT_currentSecs = FT_currentTime.getSeconds();
  FT_givenSeconds = FT_currentHours * 3600 + FT_currentMins * 60 + FT_currentSecs;
  FT_givenSeconds += secondsLeft;
  FT_getTime();
}
function FT_getTime()
{
  var FT_newCurrentTime = new Date();
  var FT_actualHours = FT_newCurrentTime.getHours();
  var FT_actualMins = FT_newCurrentTime.getMinutes();
  var FT_actualSecs = FT_newCurrentTime.getSeconds();
  FT_actualSeconds = FT_actualHours * 3600 + FT_actualMins * 60 + FT_actualSecs;
  FT_displayCountdown();
}
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            FT_getCountdown(8550);
        </script>
    
</div>

        
        <script type="text/javascript">
    P.when("A", "jQuery").execute(function(A, $) {
        $("#quantity").live("change", function (event) {
            if (event.updateFTOnQuantityChange) {
                return;
            }
            event.updateFTOnQuantityChange = 1;

            var quantity = $(this).val();
            var asin = $("#ftSelectAsin").val();
            var merchantId = $("#ftSelectMerchant").val();

            if (!asin || !merchantId) {
                return;
            }

            var params = [];
            params.push("asin=" + asin);
            params.push("quantity=" + quantity);
            params.push("merchantId=" + merchantId);

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "/gp/product/features/dp-fast-track/udp-ajax-handler/get-quantity-update-message.html?ie=UTF8",
                contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded;charset=utf-8',
                data: params.join('&'),
                dataType: "html",
                success: function(objResponse) {
                    if (objResponse != null && objResponse != "") {
                        $("#fast-track-message").replaceWith(objResponse);
                    }
                }
            });
            return;
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="a-state" data-a-state="{&quot;key&quot;:&quot;popoverState&quot;}">{"showWishListDropDown":true,"wishlistPopoverWidth":232,"showPopover":true,"isAddToWishListDropDownAuiEnabled":false,"babyRegistryId":"add-to-registry-baby-button","showBabyRegDropdown":false}</script>


    
    
        
        <script type="a-state" data-a-state="{&quot;key&quot;:&quot;popoverState&quot;}">{"showWishListDropDown":true,"wishlistPopoverWidth":232,"showPopover":true,"isAddToWishListDropDownAuiEnabled":false,"babyRegistryId":"add-to-registry-baby-button","atwlJSIncluded":true,"showBabyRegDropdown":false}</script>
        


<script type="text/javascript">
P.when('A', 'a-popover', 'cf').execute(function(A, popover) {
    
    function setRegistryId(regStr) {
        var addToCart = $("#addToCart");
        addToCart.find("[name='sourceCustomerOrgListID'],[name='colid'],[name='wlPopCommand']").attr('value', regStr);
        addToCart.find("[name='submit.add-to-registry.wishlist'],[name='submit.add-to-wishlist']").eq(0).click();
        return false;
    }
    window.setRegistryId = setRegistryId;

    function clearText(thefield){
        if (thefield.value === thefield.defaultValue) {
            thefield.value = "";
        }
    }

    
    function makeDropDownArrowInactive() {
        $('#wishListDropDown').removeClass('a-button-selected');
        $('#wishListMainButton').removeClass('a-button-selected');
    }
    
    
    function setAtwlState(options) {
        A.state('atwl', $.extend(A.state('atwl'), options));
    }
    
    function getDropDownHtml() {
        var atwlState = A.state('atwl');
        return atwlState.dropDownHtml;
    }
    
    function setDropDownHtml(dropDownHtml) {
        setAtwlState({dropDownHtml : dropDownHtml});
    }
    
    function resetDropDownHtml() {
        setDropDownHtml('');
    }
    
    function isListOverflowing() {
        var $popoverWrapper = $('#atwl-dd-ul').parent();
        if ($popoverWrapper && $popoverWrapper.get(0)) {
            var scrollHeight = $popoverWrapper.get(0).scrollHeight;
            var height = $popoverWrapper.height();
            var vertPadding = 2*parseInt($popoverWrapper.css('padding-top'), 10);
            return (scrollHeight > height + vertPadding);
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    function ie8NoScroll() {
        if (parseInt($.browser.version, 10) < 9 && document.body && document.body.parentElement) {
            return !!(document.body.parentElement.scrollLeft || document.body.parentElement.scrollTop);
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    function adjustPopover($popover) {
        $popover.find('.a-button-close').hide();
        $popover.find('.a-popover-content').css({
            'margin-right' : '0px'
        });
        $popover.css({
            'padding' : '0'
        });
        $popover.find('.a-popover-inner').css({
            'padding' : '0'
        });
        setTimeout(function () {
            $popover.removeClass('a-arrow-bottom');
            $('#atwl-rich-content').css({
                'margin-bottom' :'0px',
                'width' : 'auto'
            });
            
            if ($.browser.msie) {
                var $atwlMain = $('#' + A.state('atwl').wishlistButtonSubmitId);
                var offset = $atwlMain.offset();
                var height = $atwlMain.height();
                var left = offset.left;
                var top = offset.top + height;
                if (ie8NoScroll()) {
                    left += document.body.parentElement.scrollLeft;
                    top += document.body.parentElement.scrollTop;
                }
                var listOverflow = isListOverflowing();
                if (listOverflow) {
                    left -= 17;
                }
                $popover.css({
                    'left' : left + 'px',
                    'top' : top + 'px'
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }
    
    
    function hideStaticPopover() {
        if (basePopoverId) {
            var basePopover = popover.get(basePopoverId);
            if (basePopover) {
                basePopover.hide();
            }
        }
    }
    
    
    function showStaticPopover(holder) {
        $('#' + holder).children().first().width(CONST.widthStaticPopovers);
        hideStaticPopover();
        var basePopover = popover.get(basePopoverId);
        if (!basePopover) {
            basePopover = popover.create($('#add-to-wishlist-button-group'), {
                content : $('#' + holder).html(),
                name : 'atwl',
                skin : function(content) {return content;},
                activate : 'onmouseclick',
                width : CONST.widthStaticPopovers,
                position : 'triggerBottom'
            });
        } else {
            basePopover = popover.get(basePopoverId);
        }
        basePopover.update({
            width : CONST.widthStaticPopovers,
            content : $('#' + holder).html()
        });
        basePopoverId = basePopover.id;
        basePopover.show().updatePosition();
        var $popover = basePopover.$popover;
        adjustPopover($popover);
    }
    
    function showSpinner() {
        showStaticPopover('atwl-dd-spinner-holder');
    }
    
    function hideSpinner() {
        hideStaticPopover();
    }
    
    function showError() {
        makeDropDownArrowInactive();
        ajaxFailCount++;
        hideSpinner();
        showStaticPopover('atwl-dd-error-holder');
    }
    
    function hideError() {
        hideStaticPopover();
        return ajaxFailCount >= A.state('atwl').maxAjaxFailureCount;
    }
    
    function hideUnavail() {
        hideStaticPopover();
    }
    
    function showUnavail() {
        hideSpinner();
        hideUnavail();
        showStaticPopover('atwl-dd-unavail-holder');
    }
    
    function createDropDown() {
        var atwlPopover = popover.create($('#add-to-wishlist-button-group'), {
            content : getDropDownHtml(),
            name : 'atwl',
            skin : function(content) {return content;},
            activate : 'onmouseclick',
            position : 'triggerBottom'
        });
        return atwlPopover;
    }
    
    function adjustDropDownDimensions($popover) {
        var timeout;
        if (ie8NoScroll()) {
            timeout = 50;
        } else {
            timeout = 0;
        }
        setTimeout(function () {
            var $inner = $('#atwl-popover-inner');
            var innerWidth = $inner.width();
            var listOverflow = isListOverflowing();
            if (listOverflow) {
                innerWidth += CONST.overflowWidth;
            } else {
                $('.atwl-dd-list-name').each(function(index) {
                    var $this = $(this);
                    $this.width($this.width() + CONST.noOverflowWidth);
                });
            }
            var defaultList = $popover.find('ul li a.a-active').first();
            defaultList.css('margin-left', '1px');
            defaultList.parent().focus();
            $inner.width(innerWidth);
        }, timeout);
    }
    
    function updateDropDown(atwlPopover) {
        atwlPopover.update({
            content : getDropDownHtml(),
            width : 'auto'
        });
        atwlPopover.show();
        adjustPopover(atwlPopover.$popover);
        adjustDropDownDimensions(atwlPopover.$popover);
    }
    
    function showDropDown() {
        var atwlPopover = popover.get('atwl');
        if (atwlPopover) {
            if (atwlPopover.isActive()) {
                atwlPopover.hide();
                return;
            } else {
                
                popover.remove(atwlPopover);
            }
        } else {
            
            atwlPopover = createDropDown();
            popover.remove(atwlPopover);
        }
        atwlPopover = createDropDown();
        updateDropDown(atwlPopover);
    }
    
    function parseAjaxResponse(ajaxResponse) {
        makeDropDownArrowInactive();
        hideSpinner();
        var response;
        try {
            response = A.parseJSON(ajaxResponse);
        } catch(e) {
            showError();
            return;
        }
        if (typeof response.html !== 'undefined' && response.css !== 'undefined') {
            setDropDownHtml(response.html);
            var dropDownCSS = response.css;
            $('body').append(dropDownCSS);
            showDropDown();
        } else {
            showError();
        }
    }
    
    function setInputRegistryId(regID, regType) {
        if (typeof regType === 'undefined') {
            regType = 'wishlist';
        }
        var regStr = 'pop_' + regID + '_' + regType;
        var addToCart = $("#addToCart");
        addToCart.find("[name='sourceCustomerOrgListID'],[name='colid'],[name='wlPopCommand']").attr('value', regStr);
        setAtwlState({'inSubmit' : true});
        addToCart.find("[name='submit.add-to-registry.wishlist'],[name='submit.add-to-wishlist']").eq(0).click();
        return false;
    }
    
    
    function showKbpPromoPopover(data) {
        
        if (data && data.promoEnabled) {
            var html = data.html;
            if (html) {
                
                var kbpPromoPopover = popover.create($atwlMain.parent(), {
                    name : 'kbpPromoPopover',
                    content : html,
                    position : 'triggerBottom',
                    width : data.width
                });
                kbpPromoPopover.show().lock();
                
                A.delay(function () {
                    var state = A.state('atwl').kbpPromo;
                    var hide = !state.mouseOver;
                    if (hide) {
                        kbpPromoPopover.unlock().hide();
                        popover.remove(kbpPromoPopover);
                    } else {
                        state.countDown = true;
                    }
                    A.state('atwl', {kbpPromo : state});
                }, 10000);
            }
        }
    }
    
    var popState = A.state('popoverState');
    if (popState.showWishListDropDown || popState.showBabyRegDropdown || popState.isAddToWishListDropDownAuiEnabled || popState.showPopover) {

        
        var $ = A.$;
        if (popState.showWishListDropDown || popState.showBabyRegDropdown) {
            var dropdownIds = "#" + popState.babyRegistryId;
            if (!popState.isAddToWishListDropDownAuiEnabled) {
                dropdownIds += ", #" + A.state('atwl').wishlistButtonId;
            }
            var dropdowns = $(dropdownIds);
            dropdowns.each(function(){
                var dropdown = $(this);
                
                dropdown[0].name = "";
                if(dropdown.css("cursor") !== "not-allowed") {
                    var wlType = dropdown.attr("data-type");
                    var id = dropdown[0].id;
                    
                    var buttonWidth = popState.wishlistPopoverWidth;
                    dropdown.amazonPopoverTrigger({
                        ajaxSlideDuration: 0,
                        align: "left",
                        cacheable: true,
                        closeEventInclude: "CLICK_OUTSIDE",
                        destination: "/gp/registry/reglist-popover.html?sprited=0&type=" + wlType,
                        group: "addToWishlist",
                        loadingContent: "<div style='padding: 4px 28px;'><img src='" + window.AmazonPopoverImages.loadingBar + "'/></div>",
                        location: "bottom",
                        locationElement: "#" + id,
                        locationOffset: [-33,-5],
                        showOnHover: false,
                        skin: "<div id='wishlist-dropdown-content'><div class='ap_content'></div></div>",
                        
                        width: buttonWidth,
                        onFilled: function(popover) {
                            
                            $(document).click();
                            popover.width(buttonWidth);
                            if (window.wlPop) {
                                setTimeout(function() {
                                    window.wlPop.onFill(popover);
                                    popover.width(buttonWidth);
                                }, 0);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }
            });
        }

        
        if (popState.isAddToWishListDropDownAuiEnabled) {
            var basePopoverId;
            var ajaxFailCount = 0;
            var wireDeclaratives = A.state('atwl').wireDeclaratives;

            
            var $atwlArrow = $('#' + A.state('atwl').wishlistButtonId);
            $atwlArrow.addClass('a-declarative');
            $atwlArrow.attr('data-action', 'atwl-splitbutton-arrow');
            var $atwlMain = $('#' + A.state('atwl').wishlistButtonSubmitId);
            $atwlMain.addClass('a-declarative');
            $atwlMain.attr('data-action', 'atwl-splitbutton-main');

            
            var CONST = {
                'widthStaticPopovers' : 230,
                'overflowWidth' : 10,
                'noOverflowWidth' : 10,
                'scrollbarWidth' : 17
            };

            setAtwlState({resetDropDownHtml : resetDropDownHtml});

            
            if (!wireDeclaratives) {
                
                A.declarative('atwl-splitbutton-arrow', 'click', function (event) {
                    var $this = event.$target;
                    event.$event.preventDefault();
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        makeDropDownArrowInactive();
                    }, 0);
                    if ($this.css("cursor") === "not-allowed") {
                        return false;
                    }
                    if (hideError()) {
                        showUnavail();
                        return false;
                    }
                    var dropDownHtml = getDropDownHtml();
                    var atwlState = A.state('atwl');
                    if (!dropDownHtml || !dropDownHtml.length) {
                        showSpinner();
                        var data = event.data;
                        var urlParams = {
                            'sortMethod' : atwlState.sortMethod,
                            'type' : 'wishlist'
                        };
                        var url = '/gp/registry/atwl/popover.html?' + $.param(urlParams);
                        var params = {
                            'url' : url,
                            'cache' : false,
                            'success' : parseAjaxResponse,
                            'error' : showError
                        };
                        $.ajax(params);
                    } else {
                        showDropDown();
                    }
                    return false;
                });
                
                A.declarative('atwl-dd', 'click', function (event) {
                    event.$event.preventDefault();
                    var data = event.data;
                    setInputRegistryId(data.id, data.type);
                    return false;
                });
                
                A.declarative('atwl-kbp-landing', 'click', function (event) {
                    var data = event.data;
                    var asin = $("#addToCart").find('#ASIN').val();
                    var href = data.url;
                    href += '&asin=' + asin;
                    window.open(href);
                    return false;
                });
            }

            var atwlState = A.state('atwl');
            if (atwlState && atwlState.sortMethod === 'kbp') {
                
                A.state('atwl', {
                    kbpPromo : {
                        mouseOver : false,
                        countDown : false
                    }
                });

                
                A.ajax('/gp/toys/birthday/atwl-dpx.html', {
                    method : 'get',
                    cache : false,
                    params : {
                        isAUI : 1
                    },
                    success : showKbpPromoPopover,
                    error : function () {}
                });
                if (!wireDeclaratives) {
                    
                    A.declarative('atwl-kbp-promo-mouseover', 'mouseleave', function () {
                        var state = A.state('atwl').kbpPromo;
                        state.mouseOver = false;
                        var hide = state.countDown;
                        if (hide) {
                            var kbpPromoPopover = popover.get('kbpPromoPopover');
                            if (kbpPromoPopover) {
                                kbpPromoPopover.unlock().hide();
                                popover.remove(kbpPromoPopover);
                            }
                        }
                        A.state('atwl', {kbpPromo : state});
                    });
                    
                    A.declarative('atwl-kbp-promo-mouseover', 'mouseenter', function () {
                        var state = A.state('atwl').kbpPromo;
                        state.mouseOver = true;
                        A.state('atwl', {kbpPromo : state});
                    });
                    
                    A.on('a:popover:hide:kbpPromoPopover', function () {
                        var kbpPromoPopover = popover.get('kbpPromoPopover');
                        kbpPromoPopover.unlock().hide();
                        popover.remove(kbpPromoPopover);
                    });
                }
            }

            setAtwlState({wireDeclaratives : true});
        }

        if (popState.showPopover) {
            var parseButtonType = function (btnClicked) {
                var btnName = btnClicked.attr("name");
                var btnNameParts = btnName.split('.');
                var re1 = new RegExp('submit' + String.fromCharCode(0x5c) + '.add-to-registry' + String.fromCharCode(0x5c) + '.');
                var re2 = new RegExp('submit' + String.fromCharCode(0x5c) + '.add-to-');
                if (re1.test(btnName)) {
                    return btnNameParts[2];
                } else if (re2.test(btnName)) {
                    var parts = btnNameParts[1].split("-");
                    return parts[2];
                }
                return '';
            };

            var parsePostData = function (action, btnType) {
                var form = $('#addToCart');
                var serArr = form.serializeArray();
                var data = {};
                var wishlistState = A.state('wishlistDPState');
                $.each(serArr, function (){
                    data[this.name] = this.value;
                });
                data['itemCount'] = data.quantity;
                data['sid'] = data['session-id'];
                data['cache'] = false;
                data['url'] = wishlistState[action + 'Url'];

                if (action === 'add') {
                    data.type = btnType;
                    data.caller = "aui";
                    data.sourceVendorId = "website.wishlist.detail.add";
                    data.streaming = wishlistState.streaming;
                } else if (action === 'create') {
                    data['create_sid'] = data.sid;
                    data['create_type'] = btnType;
                    data['create_sourceVendorId'] = "website.createflow.assign";
                    data['create_nextAction'] = "add";
                    data['create_includeEmptyList'] = 1;
                    data['create_isFirst'] = wishlistState.isFirstCreate ? 1 : 0;
                    data.caller = "aui";
                }
                return data;
            };

            var forceFormSubmit = function (btnClicked) {
                var btnName = btnClicked.attr('name');
                var form = btnClicked.parents('form');
                var inputName = $('<input type="hidden" />').attr("name", btnName).val('1');
                form.append($(inputName));
                form.submit();
            };

            var redirectToHUCPage = function() {
                var btnClicked = $('#add-wishlist-declarative').closest('.a-button').find('input');
                forceFormSubmit(btnClicked);
            }

            if (!A.capabilities.touch) {
                $('#add-to-wishlist-button-submit').unbind("click").bind("click", function(event) {
                    event.preventDefault();

                    if ($(this).css("cursor") === "not-allowed") {
                        return false;
                    }

                    var currentAction = "";
                    var dpState = A.state('wishlistDPState');
                    var popCommand = $("[name='wlPopCommand']").val();
                    var currentType = window.currentType;

                    if (popCommand !== "") {
                        
                        var popCommandParts = popCommand.split('_');
                        currentType = popCommandParts[2];
                        
                        
                        if ((currentType !== 'wishlist' && currentType !== 'giftlist' && currentType !== 'supplylist') ||
                               $('html').hasClass('a-lt-ie9'))  {
                            redirectToHUCPage();
                            return;
                        }
                        currentAction = (popCommandParts[1] === 'new') ? "create" : (popCommandParts[1] === 'default' && dpState.isFirstCreate) ? "create" : "add";
                    } else {
                        currentType = "wishlist";
                        currentAction =  dpState.isFirstCreate ? "create" : "add";
                        
                        if (currentAction === "add" && $('html').hasClass('a-lt-ie9')) {
                            redirectToHUCPage();
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    A.state("wishlistDPState", {action: currentAction, type: currentType});
                    window.currentType = currentType;
                    $('#add-wishlist-declarative').trigger("click");
                });
            }


            var clearPopCommandFields = function() {
                
                var popCommandFields = ['wlPopCommand', 'sourceCustomerOrgListID'];
                for (var i = 0; i < popCommandFields.length; i++) {
                    var fieldName = popCommandFields[i];
                    var field = $('[name^="' + fieldName + '"]');
                    if (field && field.length) {
                        field.val("");
                    }
                }
            }

            var eventAlreadyBound = A.state('wishlistDPState').eventsBound;

            if (!eventAlreadyBound) {
                A.on('a:popover:show:addCreateToWishlist' , function(event) {
                    var popover = event.popover;
                    var $popover = popover.$popover;
                    var wishlistState = A.state('wishlistDPState');
                    var action = wishlistState.action;

                    $popover.addClass('pop-huc-' + action);
                    var btnClicked = popover.$trigger.closest('.a-button').find('input');
                    var btnType = wishlistState.type;
                    
                    btnClicked.closest('.a-button-selected').removeClass('a-button-selected');

                    
                    var declarativeData = parsePostData(action, btnType);
                    var url = declarativeData.url;
                    var streaming = declarativeData.streaming;
                    var scope = "ajax_" + streaming;
                    var t0 = new Date();
                    if (window.ue) {
                        window.uet('tc', scope);
                    }

                    var closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit = function() {
                        popover.hide();
                        forceFormSubmit(btnClicked);
                    };

                    var hidePopoverSpinnerWithClearFields = function() {
                        popover.$popover.find('#popover-spinner').addClass('a-hidden');
                        clearPopCommandFields();
                    }

                    var emitRawUEData = function() {
                        if (window.ue) {
                            window.uet("be", scope);
                            window.uex("ld", scope);
                        }
                    };

                    var emitCF = function() {
                        if (window.ue) {
                            window.uet("cf", scope);
                        }
                    }

                    var emitHitData = function(requestId, time, ctb) {
                        if (window.ue) {
                            window.ues("id", scope, requestId);
                            window.ues("t0", scope, time);
                            window.ues("ctb", scope, ctb);
                        }
                    };

                    if (action === "create" || !streaming) {
                        A.ajax(url, {
                            method: 'post',
                            params: declarativeData,
                            success: function(response) {
                                if (response && response.html) {
                                    emitHitData(response.requestId, t0, "1");
                                    if (response.status && response.status === 'no-asins') {
                                        
                                        closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit();
                                    } else {
                                        
                                        hidePopoverSpinnerWithClearFields();
                                        if (action === 'add') {
                                            popover.$popover.find('#WLHUC_result').html(response.html).removeClass('a-hidden');
                                        } else {
                                            popover.$popover.find('#WLNEW_main').html(response.html).removeClass('a-hidden');
                                            
                                            var wlDropDownState = A.state('atwl');
                                            if (wlDropDownState && wlDropDownState.resetDropDownHtml ) {
                                                wlDropDownState.resetDropDownHtml();
                                            }
                                        }

                                        popover.updatePosition();
                                    }
                                    emitRawUEData();
                                } else {
                                    if (action === 'create') {
                                        forceFormSubmit(btnClicked);
                                    }
                                    popover.hide();
                                }
                            },
                            error: closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit
                        });
                    } else {

                        var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
                        request.open("GET", declarativeData.url + "&" + A.$.param(declarativeData), true);
                        request.send(null);
                        var lastChunkIndex = 0;

                        request.ontimeout = closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit;

                        request.onerror = closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit;

                        request.onreadystatechange = function() {
                            try {
                                if (request.readyState > 2 && (typeof(request.status) !== "unknown" && request.status === 200) && (typeof(request.response) !== 'undefined' || (typeof(request.responseText) !== 'unknown' && typeof(request.responseText) !== 'undefined'))) {
                                    var jsons = [];
                                    if (typeof(request.response) !== 'undefined' && request.response !== null) {
                                        jsons = request.response.split(",,,");
                                    } else if (typeof(request.responseText) !== 'unknown' && typeof(request.responseText) !== 'undefined' && request.responseText !== null) {
                                        jsons = request.responseText.split(",,,");
                                    }
                                    for (var index = lastChunkIndex; index < jsons.length ; index++) {
                                        var json = jsons[index];
                                        var response;
                                        try {
                                            response = A.parseJSON(json);
                                        } catch (e) {
                                            lastChunkIndex = index;
                                            break;
                                        }
                                        if (index === 0 && response && response.name === "skeleton") {
                                            
                                            if (response && response.html) {
                                                emitHitData(response.requestId, new Date(), "1");
                                                if (response.status && response.status === 'no-asins') {
                                                    
                                                    closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit();
                                                } else {
                                                    
                                                    hidePopoverSpinnerWithClearFields();
                                                    popover.$popover.find('#WLHUC_result').html(response.html).removeClass('a-hidden');
                                                }
                                            }
                                        } else if(response && response.name && response.html && response.name !== "js") {
                                          popover.$popover.find('#' + response.name).html(response.html);
                                          
                                          if (index === 1) {
                                              emitCF();
                                          }
                                        } else if(response && response.html){
                                          popover.$popover.find('#WLHUC_result').append(response.html);
                                        }
                                        popover.updatePosition();
                                    }
                                    if (request.readyState === 4) {
                                        emitRawUEData();
                                    }
                                } else if(typeof(request.status) !== 'unknown' && request.status !== 200) {
                                    closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit();
                                }
                            } catch (e) {
                                closePopoverWithForceFormSubmit();
                            }
                        };
                    }
                });

                A.on('a:popover:beforeShow:addCreateToWishlist' , function(event) {
                    var popover = event.popover;
                    var $popover = popover.$popover;
                    var wishlistState = A.state('wishlistDPState');
                    
                    popover.$popover.find('#popover-spinner').css({'margin': '10% 40%'});
                    popover.$popover.find('#popover-spinner').removeClass('a-hidden');
                    
                    popover.$popover.find('.wlAddCreatePop').html('').addClass('a-hidden');

                    
                    var action = wishlistState.action;
                    popover.update({"width": wishlistState[action + 'Width'], "header": wishlistState[action + 'Header'], "height": wishlistState[action + 'Height']});
                    popover.updatePosition();
                });

                A.on('a:popover:hide:addCreateToWishlist' , function(event) {
                    $('.a-modal-scroller').css({"visibility":"hidden"});
                    clearPopCommandFields();
                });

                A.state("wishlistDPState", {eventsBound: true});
            }
        }
    }
});
</script>

    



    
  </form>
</div>



        
        
        
        
        
        
    
    
        
    






    </div>






        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        









        
    
        
        

        











    <div id="tradeInButton_feature_div" class="feature" data-feature-name="tradeInButton">




    

    
    
    
        
            





        
        
        
        
        
        
    
    






    </div>






        
    
        
        

        











    <div id="moreBuyingChoices_feature_div" class="feature" data-feature-name="moreBuyingChoices">

                <div class="a-box a-text-center"><div class="a-box-inner a-padding-small">
                    
                        
                        
                    
                    
                        
                        
                            <h5>Other Sellers on Amazon</h5>
                        
                    
                </div></div>
                
                
                    <div class="a-box"><div class="a-box-inner a-padding-base">
                        <span class="a-size-small a-center"><a href="/gp/offer-listing/0321751043/ref=dp_olp_all_mbc?ie=UTF8&amp;condition=all">51&nbsp;used&nbsp;&&nbsp;new</a>&nbsp;from&nbsp;<span class='a-color-price'>$169.95</span></span>
                    </div></div>

                <div class="a-section a-padding-base">
                    <span class="a-size-small sdpText">Have one to sell?</span>

                        Sell on Amazon
                    </a></span></span>

P.when('A','jQuery').execute(function(A,$)  {
	var offerCount = 0;
    for(var i=1; i <= offerCount; i++){
        $(".mbcLi"+i).bind("click", function(){
            this.click();
        });
        $(".mbcLi"+i+" .a-button a").bind("click", function(){
            window.open(this.href,"_self");
        });
    }
});


P.when("A").execute(function (A) {
     A.declarative("atozWindow", "click", function(event){
    	 window.open("/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=mbc_dp_atoz_1?ie=UTF8&nodeId=200783670&pop-up=1",null,
    	 "height=400, width=400, status=yes, toolbar=no, menubar=no, location=no");
     });
    
});
</script>

P.when("A","jQuery").execute(function(A, $) {	
	function setGalleryDimensions() {
		var ratio = 0.75,
		    $trigger = $("#imgThumbs"),
		    data = $trigger.data("a-modal"),
		    viewport = A.viewport();
		
		data.width = viewport.width * ratio;
		data.height = viewport.height * ratio;
		$trigger.data("a-modal", data);
		
	}	
	setGalleryDimensions();
	A.on("resize", setGalleryDimensions);
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
	var insertCenterColStyle = function(width) {
		var totalWidth = width + 40,
		    style = document.createElement('style'),
		    head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0],
		    css = '#centerCol.centerColumn{margin-left:' + totalWidth + 'px !important;}';
		
		style.type = 'text/css';
		if(style.styleSheet) {
			style.styleSheet.cssText = css;
		} else {
			style.appendChild(document.createTextNode(css));
		}
		head.appendChild(style);
	};

	var maintainWidth = function() {
		var w = window.innerWidth || document.body.offsetWidth;
		if(w < 1150) {	
			var containerWidth = 200,
			    containerHeight = containerWidth / 0.75,
			    leftCol = document.getElementById("leftCol"),
			    imageBlock = document.getElementById("imageBlock"),
			    imageBlockContainer = document.getElementById("imageBlockContainer"),
			    frontImage = document.getElementById("imgBlkFront"),
			    imageCanvas = document.getElementById("img-canvas");
			        
	        leftCol.style.width = containerWidth + "px";
			imageBlock.style.width = containerWidth + "px";
			imageBlock.style.height = containerHeight + 40 + "px";
			imageBlockContainer.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
	        imageCanvas.style.height = containerHeight + "px";
	        frontImage.style.overflow = "hidden";
	    }
	    insertCenterColStyle(containerWidth);   
	};
	maintainWidth();
})();

<script type="text/javascript">
P.register("DynamicIframe", function(){

function DynamicIframe(options) {
  
  var nTries = 0,
      MAX_TRIES = 20,
      iframeId = options.iframeId,
      encodedIframeContent = options.encodedIframeContent,
      iframeWrapperId = options.iframeWrapperId,
      initialResizeCallback = options.initialResizeCallback,
      iframeCSSId = "dynamic_iframe_CSS";
      iframeOverriddenCSSId = options.overriddenCSSId;
    
  this.createIframe = function() {
    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.id = iframeId;
    iframe.className = "ap_never_hide";
    iframe.width = "100%";
    iframe.scrolling = "no";
    iframe.frameBorder = "0";
    onloadFn = this.iframeload;
    
    if ( iframe.addEventListener )
      iframe.addEventListener("load", onloadFn, false);
    else if ( iframe.attachEvent )
      iframe.attachEvent("onload", onloadFn);
    else iframe.onload = onloadFn;
    
    var wrapper = document.getElementById(iframeWrapperId);
    wrapper.innerHTML = '';
    iframe = wrapper.appendChild(iframe);
    
    var overriddenCSS = "";
    if (document.getElementById(iframeOverriddenCSSId)) {
    	overriddenCSS = document.getElementById(iframeOverriddenCSSId).innerHTML;
    }
    
    var doc = iframe.contentWindow.document || iframe.contentDocument;
    if (doc && doc.open) {
      doc.open();

      doc.writeln('<html><head><base target="_top" /></' + 'head><body><style class="text/css">' + document.getElementById(iframeCSSId).innerHTML + overriddenCSS + '</style><div id="iframeContent">' + 
              '' + decodeURIComponent(encodedIframeContent) + '</'+'div>'+'</'+'body></html>');
      doc.close();
    }
  }
  
  this.iframeload = function () {
    var iframe = document.getElementById(iframeId);
    iframe.style.display = '';
    setTimeout(function () {
      setIframeHeight(initialResizeCallback);
    }, 20); 
  }
  
  function getDocHeight(doc) {
    var contentDiv = doc.getElementById("iframeContent");
    
    return Math.max(
    	contentDiv.scrollHeight,
    	contentDiv.offsetHeight,
    	contentDiv.clientHeight
    );
  }
  
  function setIframeHeight(resizeCallback) {
    var iframeDoc, iframe = document.getElementById(iframeId);
    iframeDoc = iframe.contentWindow.document || iframe.contentDocument;
    if (iframeDoc) {
      var h = getDocHeight(iframeDoc);
      if (h && h != 0) {
        iframe.style.height = parseInt(h) + 'px';
        if(typeof resizeCallback == "function") {
          resizeCallback(iframeId);	
        }
      } else if (nTries < MAX_TRIES) {
        nTries++;
        setTimeout(function () {
            setIframeHeight(resizeCallback);
        }, 50);
      }
    }
  }
  
  this.resizeIframe = function(resizeCallback) {
    nTries = 0;
	setIframeHeight(resizeCallback);
  }
}

return DynamicIframe;
});
</script>

        
        
        
        
        
        
    
    






    </div>

 	<div> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>The bible of all fundamental algorithms and the work that taught many of today&rsquo;s software developers most of what they know about computer programming.</i> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>&mdash;Byte</i>, September 1995</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">Countless readers have spoken about the profound personal influence of Knuth&rsquo;s work. Scientists have marveled at the beauty and elegance of his analysis, while ordinary programmers have successfully applied his &ldquo;cookbook&rdquo; solutions to their day-to-day problems. All have admired Knuth for the breadth, clarity, accuracy, and good humor found in his books.</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>I can&rsquo;t begin to tell you how many pleasurable hours of study and recreation they have afforded me! I have pored over them in cars, restaurants, at work, at home&hellip; and even at a Little League game when my son wasn&rsquo;t in the line-up.</i> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>&mdash;</i>Charles Long</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">Primarily written as a reference, some people have nevertheless found it possible and interesting to read each volume from beginning to end. A programmer in China even compared the experience to reading a poem.</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>If you think you&rsquo;re a really good programmer&hellip; read [Knuth&rsquo;s] </i>Art of Computer Programming<i>&hellip; You should definitely send me a r&eacute;sum&eacute; if you can read the whole thing.</i> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>&mdash;</i>Bill Gates</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">Whatever your background, if you need to do any serious computer programming, you will find your own good reason to make each volume in this series a readily accessible part of your scholarly or professional library.</p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&nbsp;</p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>It&rsquo;s always a pleasure when a problem is hard enough that you have to get the Knuths off the shelf. I find that merely opening one has a very useful terrorizing effect on computers.</i> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <i>&mdash;</i>Jonathan Laventhol</p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <br> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;">In describing the new fourth volume, one reviewer listed the qualities that distinguish all of Knuth&rsquo;s work. </p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <br> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;">[In sum:] <i>detailed coverage of the basics, illustrated with well-chosen examples; occasional forays into more esoteric topics and problems at the frontiers of research; impeccable writing peppered with occasional bits of humor; extensive collections of exercises, all with solutions or helpful hints; a careful attention to history; implementations of many of the algorithms in his classic step-by-step form.</i> <br> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;">&mdash;Frank Ruskey</p> <p style="margin: 0px;"> <br> </p> <p style="margin: 0px;">These four books comprise what easily could be the most important set of information on any serious programmer&rsquo;s bookshelf.</p></div>

P.when('DynamicIframe').execute(function(DynamicIframe){
	var BookDescriptionIframe = null,
	    bookDescEncodedData = "%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%20%3Ci%3EThe%20bible%20of%20all%20fundamental%20algorithms%20and%20the%20work%20that%20taught%20many%20of%20today%26rsquo%3Bs%20software%20developers%20most%20of%20what%20they%20know%20about%20computer%20programming.%3C%2Fi%3E%20%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%20%3Ci%3E%26mdash%3BByte%3C%2Fi%3E%2C%20September%201995%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%26nbsp%3B%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3ECountless%20readers%20have%20spoken%20about%20the%20profound%20personal%20influence%20of%20Knuth%26rsquo%3Bs%20work.%20Scientists%20have%20marveled%20at%20the%20beauty%20and%20elegance%20of%20his%20analysis%2C%20while%20ordinary%20programmers%20have%20successfully%20applied%20his%20%26ldquo%3Bcookbook%26rdquo%3B%20solutions%20to%20their%20day-to-day%20problems.%20All%20have%20admired%20Knuth%20for%20the%20breadth%2C%20clarity%2C%20accuracy%2C%20and%20good%20humor%20found%20in%20his%20books.%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%26nbsp%3B%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%20%3Ci%3EI%20can%26rsquo%3Bt%20begin%20to%20tell%20you%20how%20many%20pleasurable%20hours%20of%20study%20and%20recreation%20they%20have%20afforded%20me%21%20I%20have%20pored%20over%20them%20in%20cars%2C%20restaurants%2C%20at%20work%2C%20at%20home%26hellip%3B%20and%20even%20at%20a%20Little%20League%20game%20when%20my%20son%20wasn%26rsquo%3Bt%20in%20the%20line-up.%3C%2Fi%3E%20%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%20%3Ci%3E%26mdash%3B%3C%2Fi%3ECharles%20Long%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%26nbsp%3B%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3EPrimarily%20written%20as%20a%20reference%2C%20some%20people%20have%20nevertheless%20found%20it%20possible%20and%20interesting%20to%20read%20each%20volume%20from%20beginning%20to%20end.%20A%20programmer%20in%20China%20even%20compared%20the%20experience%20to%20reading%20a%20poem.%3C% nto%20more%20esoteric%20topics%20and%20problems%20at%20the%20frontiers%20of%20research%3B%20impeccable%20writing%20peppered%20with%20occasional%20bits%20of%20humor%3B%20extensive%20collections%20of%20exercises%2C%20all%20with%20solutions%20or%20helpful%20hints%3B%20a%20careful%20attention%20to%20history%3B%20implementations%20of%20many%20of%20the%20algorithms%20in%20his%20classic%20step-by-step%20form.%3C%2Fi%3E%20%3Cbr%3E%20%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%26mdash%3BFrank%20Ruskey%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3E%20%3Cbr%3E%20%3C%2Fp%3E%20%3Cp%20style%3D%22margin%3A%200px%3B%22%3EThese%20four%20books%20comprise%20what%20easily%20could%20be%20the%20most%20important%20set%20of%20information%20on%20any%20serious%20programmer%26rsquo%3Bs%20bookshelf.%3C%2Fp%3E",
	    bookDescriptionAvailableHeight,
	    minBookDescriptionInitialHeight = 112,
	    options = {};
	    
    function resizeCallback() {
       	var bdOffsetTop = document.getElementById("bookDescription_feature_div").offsetTop;
   		var imageBlockOffsetTop = document.getElementById("booksImageBlock_feature_div").offsetTop;
   		var imageBlockHeight = document.getElementById("booksImageBlock_feature_div").offsetHeight;
   		bookDescriptionAvailableHeight = imageBlockOffsetTop + imageBlockHeight -bdOffsetTop - 30;
   		if(bookDescriptionAvailableHeight < minBookDescriptionInitialHeight) {
   	        bookDescriptionAvailableHeight = minBookDescriptionInitialHeight;
   		}
    		
    	var psTotalHeight = document.getElementById("postBodyPS").offsetHeight;

    	if(psTotalHeight > bookDescriptionAvailableHeight + 30){
    		if(document.getElementById("bdSeeLessPrompt").style.display == "none"){
    	    	document.getElementById("outer_postBodyPS").style.height = bookDescriptionAvailableHeight + 'px';
    	    	document.getElementById("psPlaceHolder").style.display ="block";
    	    	document.getElementById("bdSeeAllPrompt").style.display ="block";
    		}
    		else{
    			document.getElementById("outer_postBodyPS").style.height = psTotalHeight + 'px';
    		}
        }
        else{
        	document.getElementById("outer_postBodyPS").style.height = psTotalHeight + 'px';
        	document.getElementById("psPlaceHolder").style.display ="none";
        	document.getElementById("bdSeeAllPrompt").style.display ="block";
	    	document.getElementById("bdSeeLessPrompt").style.display ="none";
	    	document.getElementById("bdExpanderIcon").className = document.getElementById("bdExpanderIcon").className.replace("rotate","");
        }
    }
	    
	options.iframeId = "bookDesc_iframe";
	options.iframeWrapperId = "bookDesc_iframe_wrapper";
	options.overriddenCSSId = "bookDesc_override_CSS";
	options.encodedIframeContent = bookDescEncodedData;
	options.initialResizeCallback = resizeCallback;
	
	BookDescriptionIframe = new DynamicIframe(options);
	BookDescriptionIframe.createIframe();
	    
	if ((typeof BookDescriptionIframe != 'undefined') && (BookDescriptionIframe instanceof DynamicIframe)) {
	  P.when('jQuery').execute(function($) {
	    $(window).resize(function() {
	        BookDescriptionIframe.resizeIframe(resizeCallback);
	    });
	    $(window).bind('imageResize', function() {
	    	BookDescriptionIframe.resizeIframe(resizeCallback);
	    });
	  });
	}
});
</script>

      function acrPopoverHover(e, h) {
        if(h) window.acrAsinHover = e;
        else if(window.acrAsinHover == e) window.acrAsinHover = null;
      }

  amznJQ.onReady('popover', function() {
    (function($) {
      if($.fn.acrPopover) return;
      var popoverConfig = {
        showOnHover:true,
        showCloseButton: true,
        width: null,
        location:'bottom',
        locationAlign:'left',
        locationOffset:[-20,0],
        paddingLeft: 15,
        paddingBottom: 5,
        paddingRight: 15,
        group: 'reviewsPopover',
        clone:false,
        hoverHideDelay:300
      };

      $.fn.acrPopover = function() {
          return this.each(function() {
            var $this = $(this);
            if(!$this.data('init') && typeof $this.amazonPopoverTrigger === 'function') {
              $this.data('init', 1);
              var getargs = $this.attr('getargs');
              var ajaxURL = '/gp/customer-reviews/common/du/displayHistoPopAjax.html?' +
                         '&ASIN=' + $this.attr('name') +
                         '&link=1' +
                         '&seeall=1' +
                         '&ref=' + $this.attr('ref') +
                         ((typeof getargs != 'undefined') ? ('&getargs=' + getargs) : '');
              var myConfig = $.extend(true, { destination: ajaxURL }, popoverConfig);
              $this.amazonPopoverTrigger(myConfig);

              var w = window.acrAsinHover;
              if(w && $(w).parents('.asinReviewsSummary').get(0) == this) {
                $this.trigger('mouseover.amzPopover');
                window.acrAsinHover = null;
              }
            }
        });
      };

      window.reviewHistPopoverConfig = popoverConfig;
      var jqInit = window.jQueryInitHistoPopovers = function(asin) {
        if (typeof $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover === 'function') {
          $('.acr-popover[name=' + asin + ']').acrPopover();
        }
      };
      window.doInit_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onAjaxUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdate_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;
      window.onCacheUpdateReselect_average_customer_reviews = jqInit;

      amznJQ.onCompletion('amznJQ.criticalFeature', function() {
          setTimeout(function() { amznJQ.declareAvailable('acrPopover'); }, 10);
      });
    })(jQuery);
  });
  amznJQ.onReady('acrPopover', function() {

      if (typeof jQuery(this).acrPopover === 'function') {

      }

<script type="text/javascript">
var ProductDescriptionIframeResize = {};
(function () {
  var d = document;
  var obj = this;
  var nTries = 1;
  var hasCustomWidth = 0;
  var MAX_TRIES = 20;
  obj.iframeId = 'product-description-iframe';
  obj.appendTo = 'iframe-wrapper';
  function getDocHeight (doc) {
    var contentDiv = doc.getElementById("pdIframeContent");
    return Math.max(
      contentDiv.scrollHeight,
      contentDiv.offsetHeight,
      contentDiv.clientHeight
    );
  }
  function isElementOnRight(pdRef, el) {
    var ret=0;
    try {
      if(pdRef, el) {
        if((el.offsetTop < pdRef.offsetTop) && (el.offsetTop + el.offsetHeight > pdRef.offsetTop)) {
          ret = 1;
        }
      }
    } catch (e) {}
    return ret;
  }
  function setWidth(iframeRef, el) {
    var elLeft, w, minW = 450;
    try {
      elLeft = el.offsetLeft;
      w = elLeft - 50;
      if(w > minW) {
        iframeRef.style.width = w + 'px';
        hasCustomWidth = 1;
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  function setIframeWidth(ifrmId) {
    var iframeRef = d.getElementById(ifrmId),
        pdRef = d.getElementById("pd-available"),
        rightCol = d.getElementById("rightCol"),
        rightRail = d.getElementById("rightRail");
    if(isElementOnRight(pdRef, rightRail)) {
      setWidth(iframeRef, rightRail); 
    } else if (isElementOnRight(pdRef, rightCol)) {
      setWidth(iframeRef, rightCol);
    }
  }
  function setIframeHeight (ifrmId) {
    var iframeDoc, iframeRef = d.getElementById(ifrmId);
    try {
      iframeDoc = iframeRef.contentWindow.document;
    } catch (e) {
      try {
        iframeDoc = iframeRef.contentDocument;
      } catch (ex) {}
    }
    if (iframeDoc) {
      var h = getDocHeight(iframeDoc);
      if (h != 0) {
        iframeRef.style.height = h + 'px';
      } else { 
        if (nTries < MAX_TRIES) {
          nTries++;
          setTimeout(function () {
            setIframeHeight(ifrmId);
          }, 50); 
        }
      }
    }
  }
  obj.iframeload = function () {
    var iframe = d.getElementById(obj.iframeId);
    iframe.style.display = '';
    iframe.style.height = "1px";
    setTimeout(function () {
      if(obj.needWidthAdjust) {
        setIframeWidth(obj.iframeId);
      }
      setIframeHeight(obj.iframeId);
      var onloadCallback = obj.onloadCallback;
      if(typeof onloadCallback === "function") {
        onloadCallback();
      }
    }, 50); 

  }
  obj.createIframe = function ( iframeId, onloadFn ) {
    var iframe = d.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.id = iframeId;
    iframe.className = "ap_never_hide";
    iframe.width = "100%";
    iframe.scrolling="no";
    iframe.frameBorder="0";
    if ( iframe.addEventListener )
      iframe.addEventListener("load", onloadFn, false);
    else if ( iframe.attachEvent )
      iframe.attachEvent("onload", onloadFn);
    else iframe.onload = onloadFn;
    return iframe; 
  }
  obj.initialize = function (onloadCallback, needWidthAdjust) {
    var iframeContent = <div id="revMHRL" class="a-section"> 


























<div id="rev-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2HRJ8QVS9AOQ2" class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary">428 of 527 people found the following review helpful</span><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2HRJ8QVS9AOQ2/ref=cm_cr_dp_title?ie=UTF8&ASIN=0321751043&nodeID=283155&store=books"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R2HRJ8QVS9AOQ2/ref=cm_cr_dp_title?ie=UTF8&ASIN=0321751043&nodeID=283155&store=books"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Beautiful books</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">






  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/AZ7ESNLZ5MVDZ/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">A. Howard</a>
  </span>
<span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on September 1, 2011</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2HRJ8QVS9AOQ2" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Hardcover<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">
    Verified Purchase
  </span>





<div class="a-section">
  Since reviews of the book content can be found elsewhere, I thought I'd review the actual collection that I bought - these four books and the box that they came in.<br><br>They are beautiful, the off-white coloured dust jackets make a pleasing change to the other pure white books that I have on my desk, and the box sets the set apart from everything else.<br><br>Also, since purchasing this set, the following things have happened.<br><br>1) My IQ increased by 1 point as soon as I placed the box on my bookshelf<br>2) The Women in my IT department increased their rating of me by 1.5.  Apparently I'm now an 8 (9 if I take my glasses off) my colleagues report that this is a 0.5 increase in rating over a non-boxed collection of these books.<br>3) I have found that taking one book out, opening to a random page and inhaling deeply, when combined with a double-shot coffee, will ensure good spirits and coding karma for at least the next 4 hours.<br><br>My only complaint about this set is the fact that they are fairly snugly fit in the box.  this requires actually tipping the box forward to select a book, you cannot fit your finger over the top of any one book to pull it out.  The exaggerated action of doing this, however invokes jealous looks and dreamy eyes from my male and female/gay colleagues respectively so is worth it.<br><br>in short:  buy this set!

<div class="a-section">
  Dr. Yale Patt once told me that anybody who reads through these volumes and completes all the exercises will become an incredibly valuable software developer, and thinker in general.  After spending a few weeks with these books, I realize that he was correct, although completing all of the exercises may be impossible in any reasonable amount of time.<br><br>Do yourself a favor.  Buy these books, read through them, and try to complete the exercises.  I promise you will become a significantly better programmer, regardless of your current skill level.
</div>

  <span class="a-size-normal">
    <span class="a-color-secondary">
      By
    </span>
    <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/A2DOQEM40CIZTQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp" class="noTextDecoration">Pradeep Sekar</a>

<span class="a-color-secondary"> on May 28, 2011</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3CZEDT5YH7DIE" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Format: Hardcover<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">
    Verified Purchase
  </span>





<div class="a-section">
  I had read Knuth in college a couple of decades ago, as part of a course. Reading the books again after all these year, without the academic pressure - Just curling up in bed, on a Saturday afternoon, opening just about any chapter, marveling at the sheer beauty of the algorithms Knuth has put together, and the way Knuth has put them together - is such a pleasure<br><br>This set is sure to be a standard reference book on your wall. I bought mine because of that last volume, which was not available in the book store near me. I plan to take my time to read through volumes 1-3, at leisure over the next several weekends, when I get a few hours to spare at home, before I hit that last volume.<br><br>I was expecting a book with a good glossy cover (talk about judging a book by its cover!). The contents are simply fabulous, and the print quality and the paper inside are great.
</div>

</div>

    var self = this,
    data = {};
    var isBooksUdploggingDisabled = false;
    var enableNewCSMs = false;
    var newCSMs = ["ma-books-image-ftb-shown","ma-books-image-listen-shown","ma-img-gallery-opened","ma-img-gallery-zoom","ma-img-gallery-thumb"];

    enableNewCSMs = true;

    self.logImpression = function(key) {
      if(!(isBooksUdploggingDisabled && controlledLogging !== undefined && controlledLogging)){
          var isNewCSM = self.isKeyNewCSM(key);
          if(!isNewCSM || ( isNewCSM && enableNewCSMs)){
              data[key]=1;
              setTimeout( self.upload, 2000 ); // upload client side metrics after 2secs of recording it.
          }
      } 
    };

      var isNewCSM = false;

              isNewCSM = true;
          }
      });
      return isNewCSM;

        (new Image()).src = url;
      }
    };

    if(forceUpload) {
        jQuery(window).unload(function() { self.upload();});
    }
};
